What a great place for authentic tacos!!
So so good I wish my stomach could fit more!
We ordered 5 Asada & 2 carnitas tacos. Man I can't tell you how good they were!
This is a taco truck on inclosed parking lot with nice, clean, covered seating area. They even have a super clean bathroom! Truck ladies are very friendly too.

I don't know what is up with all the negative reviews on here, it's a shame that people are ruining it for others.
Spread your negativity somewhere else.

Bottom line, go check em out for your self!
Thank you for a tasty dinner taco truck ladies!< /text>

< Text>
This church does not allow taking pictures or video close to the seats, they only allow pictures and video from the second floor.  So, if you are trying to record memories of baptism, funeral, or wedding, you have to look somewhere else where they allow cameras close to the seats and not from the second floor.

< review>
After working in a amazing bakery in south orange county I have become very picky about my cakes. I was skeptical and nervous about this place because they had so many vegan options. We hired Jamaica to make our wedding cake, and it was such a great decision in so many ways. We had a semi-naked chocolate cake with white chocolate frosting, and a strawberry mousse and whipped cream filling, and just typing those words makes me want to eat it all again.

But let‚Äôs be honest, the two things you probably care most about are:
Q. Did it look beautiful? A. YES
Q. Was it delicious? A. HELL YES

On top of that Jamaica herself was really helpful while we were organising it all. She was always happy to suggest practical and tasty combinations to fit our vague notions of what we wanted from a cake; she prepared a tasting selection for us to take home and enjoy as part of the most delicious breakfast I‚Äôve ever had, and she went out of her way to accommodate a couple of very specific requests we had.

In conclusion, if you want a fabulous wedding cake, I STRONGLY recommend Jamaica.<//Review>

I go to this Ralph's often ( I can walk to it, so it's very convenient.) They can be a bit pricy,  but if you go for their weekly specials and deals you can do pretty well!  I really like when they have their Progresso Soup on sale. I've seen stores list the soup up to $3.49 or more, per can, retail. Winter days and nights are great for having your favorite soup, complimented with your favorite grilled cheese, or even a good salad. It's comfort food that's good for you!  And if you're not familiar with they're  "clearanced" bakery goods, or  their manager's   "specials"   on seafood and/or meat in their Butcher's Dept. then please look for them in your neighborhood Ralph's. < review>
Stopped in on Saturday evening for dinner. Had a great experience. Tried the ribs, pulled pork, and the brisket. Ribs were tasty with just right flavor and a little stickiness to the glaze, just right. Pulled pork celebrates the pork. You can add sauce to your taste but it comes straight off of the smoker with just the rub and the bark. I love that they have nothing to hide, I want to taste the pork shoulder before I sauce it and this was wonderful. And the brisket... Outstanding! Would I like a bit more bark, Yes. Do I prefer a bit more spice, Yes. But if I want to please just me then I should cook it myself. These guys are making fantastic Q way up on the NorCal coast and they can hang with anything I have had in CA. This is not EXACTLY central TX bbq but we're not in central TX.

The creamy slaw was really good and would be welcome at any church picnic. The poppers are fun with a little something extra in the cream cheese. Definitely worth trying a few. AND... the deviled eggs are worth the drive all by themselves. Now I'm not saying we snuck in a bottle of bourbon and paired it with the porkbelly topped eggs. But if we had, I bet it would have been Out Of This World! ( okay, We did. )

So why only 4 stars? Well, I try to take these notes pretty seriously and the food and service were 5 star all the way. The seating and decor are plain and a little cafeteria like. Very clean and I look forward to returning when they have made a ton of money and can put a few dollars into sprucing the place up. Please don't hold that against them. This is a great place that I look forward to again the next time I am this far north.< /review>

< text>
Not very good.  The mac and cheese was thick and flavorless, the meat tasted ok but was dry and chewy.  Their BBQ sauces didn't really help, too sweet, not much going on with it.  The spicy coleslaw was kind of like cabbage that had been tossed in Italian dressing then had a ton of vinegar added to it.  Maybe see if they'll let you taste a bit of it before you order it.  I certainly wouldn't have ordered it if I had tried it first.  I'm not one to leave things uneaten, but I couldn't stomach that slaw.</text>

< review>
I read some reviews on that other site (which I won't name) and everyone raved about their BBQ.  I had their smoked ribs, nothing to write home about, the meat didn't have the slight chewiness that I like with my  pork ribs, but it also wasn't fall off the bone good either.  The BBQ sauce it came with was pretty generic.  They said the sauce was spicy but no hint of heat any where.  I also got the Jalapeno poppers which was half a grilled jalapeno stuff with cream cheese and topped with bacon bits.  One was had heat while the other wasn't spicy at all.  I also tried the deviled egg topped with pork belly, the egg lacked season and the pork belly wasn't enough to give it the pop.  The service here is good and friendly, don't come too late because they start running out of stuff.<//review>
